<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлекать.html>увлека́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvlekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлекаться.html>увлека́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvlekátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечься.html>увле́чься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take an interest in</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ув<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:увлечься.html>увле́чься</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-влек-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увлекать.html>увлека́ющий</a> (11449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">увле́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvlék-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увлечься.html>увле́чься</a> (6802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечь.html>увле́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvléčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечься.html>увле́чься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvléčʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлекаться.html>увлека́ться</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be carried away with, to take a great interest in</li>
<li>to take a fancy to, to be infatuated with, to fall for</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увлечь.html>увле́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvléčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ув<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>ле́чь</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***увольнять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увольнять.html>увольня́ть</a> (18023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уволить.html>уво́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvólitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with unexpected interpolation of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-н-</span> influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вольный.html>во́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vólʹnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увольнять.html>увольня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvolʹnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уволить.html>уво́лить</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увы.html>увы́</a> (2432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wai</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">woe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vae</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">vaĩ</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उवे</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hittite_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hittite language">Hittite</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hit-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uwai</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">وای</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vây</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvjádšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>withered, faded, sere, sapless, flaccid, dead <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">about flowers, trees, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стья</a> — <i>induvia, induviae</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">faded, but not abscised</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uvjádšije</b> cvetý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dead flowers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uvjádšaja</b> róza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">withered rose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lost youth, freshness, beauty; passé
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uvjádšeje</b> licó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">autumnal face</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красотка.html>красо́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uvjádšije</b> krasótki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">faded beauties</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:увядший.html>увя́дшая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uvjádšaja</b> kóža</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wizened skin</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> slacken, drooping</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a> (13953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязывать.html>увя́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to pack up, to strap</li>
<li>to coordinate <i>(with)</i>, to harmonize <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to get the agreement <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to link <i>(to)</i>, to make conditional <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a> (19277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjáznutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvjáznutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́зла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašína <b>uvjázla</b> v grjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car (got) stuck in the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get bogged down <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долга́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po úši <b>uvjáznutʹ</b> v dolgáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be up to the neck in debt</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
